***потихоньку.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потихоньку.html>потихо́ньку</a> (4006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тихий.html>ти́хий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tíxij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-оньку</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-onʹku</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потихоньку.html>потихо́ньку</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potixónʹku</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>OK, so-so (in answer to the question, "<a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела</a>?" ("How are you?"), the response "<a href = vnd.unilang:потихоньку.html>потихо́ньку</a>"—"OK" or "I'm getting along okay"—implies that things could be better and could be worse)</li>
<li>silently</li>
<li>gently</li>
<li>on the sly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тихий.html>ти́хий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tíxij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тихо.html>ти́хо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tíxo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потный.html>по́тный</a> (4974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пот.html>пот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потный.html>по́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pótnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)потне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)потне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sweaty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:потный.html>по́тные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pótnyje</b> noskí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sweaty socks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>Тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потный.html>по́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувак.html>чува́к</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>брат</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tot <b>pótnyj</b> čuvák — moj brat.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">That sweaty dude is my brother.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́к</a> (1694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*potokъ</i>. Morphologically <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>ток</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>tok</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stream</li>
<li>torrent</li>
<li>flow</li>
<li>assembly line production</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thread</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a form of punishment in the medieval Russia when a criminal was exiled and property was confiscated, later the criminal was enslaved and property given away</li></ol>

***потолок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a> (1409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tьlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ground, bottom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*telh₂-o-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*telh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bear, carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">तल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">surface, bottom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tellūs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ground, land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potolók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потолка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потолки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потолко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ceiling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плевать.html>плева́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plevátʹ v potolók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit around doing nothing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потолка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ s potolká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make up, to spin out of thin air</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> upper limit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> limit in someone's development</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> roof</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́м</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ствен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***потому.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> (120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">according to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tot</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potomú</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>therefore, because of that, consequently</li></ol>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i <b>potomú</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i>and consequently</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl>

***потонуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потонуть.html>потону́ть</a> (14708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tonútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потонуть.html>потону́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potonútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонуть.html>тону́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потопать.html>потопа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sink, to go down</li>
<li>to drown</li>
<li>to be lost</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>to sink

<li>to ruin, to destroy

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́ть</a> (18463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toropítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potoropítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurry, to hasten, to precipitate, to rush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>potoropítʹ</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hurry someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>potoropíl</b> menjá s okončánijem rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is hurried me to finish my work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>potoropíl</b> menjá s otvétom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he hurried/pressed me for an answer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>potoropítʹ</b> sobýtija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush things</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">потре́ба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potréba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребный.html>потре́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrébnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)потре́бнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)потре́бней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>necessary, required, needed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:потребный.html>потре́бное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́чество</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>potrébnoje</b> kolíčestvo ljudéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>required</b> number of people</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́боваться</a> (4201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребовать.html>потре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potrébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́боваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrébovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требоваться.html>тре́боваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to need, to require
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́буется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:программист.html>программи́ст</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam <b>potrébujetsja</b> programmíst.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We will <b>need</b> a programmer.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take (time, effort, money, etc. for something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́буется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na éto <b>potrébujetsja</b> mnógo vrémeni.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It will <b>take</b> a lot of time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
